This is the project idea.

 POROLYTICS — OPPONENT PLAYBOOK (FULL MECHANICS)

Porolytics converts raw match telemetry into decision-level intelligence.

 Every section below is derived from the same underlying state graph, just queried differently.

1️⃣ TEAM IDENTITY

🎯 What this answers

How does this team fundamentally want to win games?

📊 Data used

Gold distribution per role over time

Objective participation by role

Fight participation by role

Lane priority states

Win vs loss correlation per role

⚙️ Process

Role Impact Scoring

For each role, compute:

% of fights involved

% of objectives involved

resource share (gold/xp)

win correlation

Dominance detection

Highest impact role pair → Primary win condition

Second highest → Secondary plan

Sacrificed lane detection

Lane with:

lowest gold share

lowest roam support

highest death tolerance in wins

📦 Final deliverable

Team Identity

 • Primary win condition: Jungle–Mid tempo

 • Secondary plan: Bot scaling

 • Sacrificed lane: Top

2️⃣ WINNING RECIPE (ACO PATH)

🎯 What this answers

What exact macro sequence do they repeat when they win?

📊 Data used

State graph (attribute vectors)

Transitions occurring in wins only

Objective timings

Spell availability states

⚙️ Process

Filter matches → wins only

Run Ant Colony Optimization on the coordination graph

Reinforce paths that:

occur frequently

lead to objectives or winning fights

Extract:

most reinforced path (primary)

secondary fallback path

📦 Final deliverable

Winning Recipe

 Bot priority → Jungle hover → Flash-synced dragon fight

This is the team’s comfort sequence.

3️⃣ VISION SYSTEM SUMMARY

🎯 What this answers

How do they see the map — and when does that system fail?

📊 Data used

Ward placements & clears

Control ward usage

Ward zones (river / jungle / lane)

Timing relative to objectives

Vision presence during fights

Win vs loss comparison

⚙️ Process

Zone-based aggregation

Count wards by map region

Objective setup check

Was vision established before spawn?

Vision-to-fight conversion

Do fights only occur with vision?

Collapse detection

Vision drop before losses

📦 Final deliverable

Vision System

 • Heavy river vision before dragon

 • Weak top-side vision

 • Vision collapses when behind before second objective

No maps shown — just conclusions.

4️⃣ ROAMING SYSTEM (MID / JG / SUPP / TP)

🎯 What this answers

How do they create numbers advantages?

📊 Data used

Player positions over time

Lane exit events

Arrival times to skirmishes

Jungle proximity

TP cast times

⚙️ Process

Roam detection

Player leaves lane polygon

Initiator identification

Who leaves first?

Synchronization scoring

Time difference between arrivals

TP classification

TP before fight = proactive

TP after fight = reactive

📦 Final deliverable

Roaming System

 • Support initiates roams

 • Jungle follows within ~8s

 • Mid roams only with jungle proximity

 • TP is mostly reactive

5️⃣ SUMMONER SPELL DEPENDENCY

🎯 What this answers

How reliant are they on spells to commit to fights?

📊 Data used

Flash & TP usage

Spell cooldown states

Fight timestamps

Win/loss outcomes

⚙️ Process

Conditional filtering

Compare fights with spells up vs down

Dependency ratio

% of fights with ≥N spells available

Synchronization check

Were spells aligned across roles?

📦 Final deliverable

Summoner Dependency

 • Flash-dependent team

 • Avoids fights without ≥3 Flashes

 • TP synchronization is inconsistent

6️⃣ LOSING RECIPE (DEFEAT ANALYSIS)

🎯 What this answers

What usually goes wrong first when they lose?

📊 Data used

Loss-only state transitions

Vision failures

Early deaths

Spell desync

Objective contest failures

⚙️ Process

Two layers:

A. Loss-path discovery

Run ACO on losses only

Find dominant collapse path

B. Attribution scoring

Compare win vs loss frequencies

Identify biggest deltas

📦 Final deliverable

Losing Recipe

 Vision setup failure → Jungler death → Forced mid fight

7️⃣ LYNCHPIN DEPENDENCY (MAX FLOW)

🎯 What this answers

What single dependency holds their entire strategy together?

📊 Data used

Winning recipe path

Role coordination reliability

Vision reliability

Spell availability consistency

⚙️ Process

Convert winning path → flow graph

Nodes = roles & systems

Edges = coordination & resource transfer

Capacities = reliability scores

Run Edmonds–Karp

Remove edges one by one → measure flow drop

📦 Final deliverable

Lynchpin

 Jungle–Mid coordination is the primary bottleneck

8️⃣ BREAK STRATEGY

🎯 What this answers

How do we break their plan in practice?

📊 Data used

Lynchpin edge

Losing recipe

Spell dependency

Timing windows

⚙️ Process

Rule-based reasoning:

If lynchpin = X

And losses correlate with Y

Then break strategy = Z

📦 Final deliverable

Break Strategy

 Force early skirmishes to burn mid/jg Flash before first dragon

9️⃣ DRAFT & GAMEPLAN ADVICE

🎯 What this answers

How do we prepare in champ select and early game?

📊 Data used

Team identity

Roam system

Vision habits

Lynchpin

⚙️ Process

Template-based mapping:

Identity → archetype denies

Lynchpin → lane pressure

Losing triggers → early plan

📦 Final deliverable

Draft & Gameplan

 • Deny roaming mid champions

 • Draft early skirmishers

 • Pressure bot side before first dragon

Now I need a way to get all the necessary data from the grid api for this winning project.
